on Jul 22 2014,2014-05-22,2014-07-23,SRA,pronucleus,Homo sapiens,developmental stage: zygote;	molecule subtype: MspI digested and bisulfite treated genomic DNA,genomic DNA,,,"For RRBS samples, cells or embryos were directely picked into the lysis buffer which contained protease to release the naked DNAs. For WGBS samples, genomic DNAs were extracted from the embryos using the Dneasy Blood & Tissue Kit (Qiagen). And for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted using the RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen).;	For RRBS samples, cells were picked into the lysis buffer to release naked DNA; then the released DNAs were digested with MspI, then filled-in and tailed with an extra ""A"" , then ligated with Illumina indexed adaptors. Bisulfite conversion was performed under the manufacturerâ€™s instructions of the MethyCode DNA Methylation Kit (Invitrogen) with minor modification, the converted DNAs were enriched by two rounds of PCR amplifications and size-selected after running 12% native polyacrylamide TBE gel. For WGBS samples, DNAs isolated from the embryos were sonicated into small fragments, then the endsof the DNAs were blunted, dA-tailed and ligated with the premethylated adapters. Then the ligated DNAs were bisulfite-converted and amplified. As for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted from the postimplantation embryos using RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen), and RNA sequencing libraries were constructed under the standard protocol of illumina. The quality-ensured libraries were used for pair-ended deep sequencing on Illumina HiSeq2000 Sequencer.",,,,,,,,,,,,"Illumina CASAVA version 1.8 were used to the basecalling.;	Reads were trimmed to remove the adapter sequences and low quality bases.;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, bisulfite-converted reads were aligned to the reference genome (hg19) using Bismark software (version 0.7.0). For the RNA-Seq samples, cleaned reads were mapped to the reference genome (hg19) using BWA tools (version 0.6.2-r126).;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, the DNA methylation levels of the cytosines (in CpG, CHH or CHG context) were estimated using comstomized Perl scripts. While the genes expression levels were calculated using the comtomized Perl scripts.;	Genome_build: hg19;	Supplementary_files_format_and_content: For RRBS and WGBS samples, the processed txt files include the DNA methylation levels of cytosines in CpG, CHH and CHG context. or embryos were directely picked into the lysis buffer which contained protease to release the naked DNAs. For WGBS samples, genomic DNAs were extracted from the embryos using the Dneasy Blood & Tissue Kit (Qiagen). And for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted using the RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen).;	For RRBS samples, cells were picked into the lysis buffer to release naked DNA; then the released DNAs were digested with MspI, then filled-in and tailed with an extra ""A"" , then ligated with Illumina indexed adaptors. Bisulfite conversion was performed under the manufacturerâ€™s instructions of the MethyCode DNA Methylation Kit (Invitrogen) with minor modification, the converted DNAs were enriched by two rounds of PCR amplifications and size-selected after running 12% native polyacrylamide TBE gel. For WGBS samples, DNAs isolated from the embryos were sonicated into small fragments, then the endsof the DNAs were blunted, dA-tailed and ligated with the premethylated adapters. Then the ligated DNAs were bisulfite-converted and amplified. As for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted from the postimplantation embryos using RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen), and RNA sequencing libraries were constructed under the standard protocol of illumina. The quality-ensured libraries were used for pair-ended deep sequencing on Illumina HiSeq2000 Sequencer.",,,,,,,,,,,,"Illumina CASAVA version 1.8 were used to the basecalling.;	Reads were trimmed to remove the adapter sequences and low quality bases.;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, bisulfite-converted reads were aligned to the reference genome (hg19) using Bismark software (version 0.7.0). For the RNA-Seq samples, cleaned reads were mapped to the reference genome (hg19) using BWA tools (version 0.6.2-r126).;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, the DNA methylation levels of the cytosines (in CpG, CHH or CHG context) were estimated using comstomized Perl scripts. While the genes expression levels were calculated using the comtomized Perl scripts.;	Genome_build: hg19;	Supplementary_files_format_and_content: For RRBS and WGBS samples, the processed txt files include the DNA methylation levels of cytosines in CpG, CHH and CHG context. Bisulfite conversion was performed under the manufacturerâ€™s instructions of the MethyCode DNA Methylation Kit (Invitrogen) with minor modification, the converted DNAs were enriched by two rounds of PCR amplifications and size-selected after running 12% native polyacrylamide TBE gel. For WGBS samples, DNAs isolated from the embryos were sonicated into small fragments, then the endsof the DNAs were blunted, dA-tailed and ligated with the premethylated adapters. Then the ligated DNAs were bisulfite-converted and amplified. As for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted from the postimplantation embryos using RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen), and RNA sequencing libraries were constructed under the standard protocol of illumina. The quality-ensured libraries were used for pair-ended deep sequencing on Illumina HiSeq2000 Sequencer.",,,,,,,,,,,,"Illumina CASAVA version 1.8 were used to the basecalling.;	Reads were trimmed to remove the adapter sequences and low quality bases.;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, bisulfite-converted reads were aligned to the reference genome (hg19) using Bismark software (version 0.7.0). For the RNA-Seq samples, cleaned reads were mapped to the reference genome (hg19) using BWA tools (version 0.6.2-r126).;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, the DNA methylation levels of the cytosines (in CpG, CHH or CHG context) were estimated using comstomized Perl scripts. While the genes expression levels were calculated using the comtomized Perl scripts.;	Genome_build: hg19;	Supplementary_files_format_and_content: For RRBS and WGBS samples, the processed txt files include the DNA methylation levels of cytosines in CpG, CHH and CHG context. Bisulfite conversion was performed under the manufacturerâ€™s instructions of the MethyCode DNA Methylation Kit (Invitrogen) with minor modification, the converted DNAs were enriched by two rounds of PCR amplifications and size-selected after running 12% native polyacrylamide TBE gel. For WGBS samples, DNAs isolated from the embryos were sonicated into small fragments, then the endsof the DNAs were blunted, dA-tailed and ligated with the premethylated adapters. Then the ligated DNAs were bisulfite-converted and amplified. As for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted from the postimplantation embryos using RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen), and RNA sequencing libraries were constructed under the standard protocol of illumina. The quality-ensured libraries were used for pair-ended deep sequencing on Illumina HiSeq2000 Sequencer.",,,,,,,,,,,,"Illumina CASAVA version 1.8 were used to the basecalling.;	Reads were trimmed to remove the adapter sequences and low quality bases.;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, bisulfite-converted reads were aligned to the reference genome (hg19) using Bismark software (version 0.7.0). For the RNA-Seq samples, cleaned reads were mapped to the reference genome (hg19) using BWA tools (version 0.6.2-r126).;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, the DNA methylation levels of the cytosines (in CpG, CHH or CHG context) were estimated using comstomized Perl scripts. While the genes expression levels were calculated using the comtomized Perl scripts.;	Genome_build: hg19;	Supplementary_files_format_and_content: For RRBS and WGBS samples, the processed txt files include the DNA methylation levels of cytosines in CpG, CHH and CHG context. Bisulfite conversion was performed under the manufacturerâ€™s instructions of the MethyCode DNA Methylation Kit (Invitrogen) with minor modification, the converted DNAs were enriched by two rounds of PCR amplifications and size-selected after running 12% native polyacrylamide TBE gel. For WGBS samples, DNAs isolated from the embryos were sonicated into small fragments, then the endsof the DNAs were blunted, dA-tailed and ligated with the premethylated adapters. Then the ligated DNAs were bisulfite-converted and amplified. As for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted from the postimplantation embryos using RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen), and RNA sequencing libraries were constructed under the standard protocol of illumina. The quality-ensured libraries were used for pair-ended deep sequencing on Illumina HiSeq2000 Sequencer.",,,,,,,,,,,,"Illumina CASAVA version 1.8 were used to the basecalling.;	Reads were trimmed to remove the adapter sequences and low quality bases.;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, bisulfite-converted reads were aligned to the reference genome (hg19) using Bismark software (version 0.7.0). For the RNA-Seq samples, cleaned reads were mapped to the reference genome (hg19) using BWA tools (version 0.6.2-r126).;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, the DNA methylation levels of the cytosines (in CpG, CHH or CHG context) were estimated using comstomized Perl scripts. While the genes expression levels were calculated using the comtomized Perl scripts.;	Genome_build: hg19;	Supplementary_files_format_and_content: For RRBS and WGBS samples, the processed txt files include the DNA methylation levels of cytosines in CpG, CHH and CHG context. Bisulfite conversion was performed under the manufacturerâ€™s instructions of the MethyCode DNA Methylation Kit (Invitrogen) with minor modification, the converted DNAs were enriched by two rounds of PCR amplifications and size-selected after running 12% native polyacrylamide TBE gel. For WGBS samples, DNAs isolated from the embryos were sonicated into small fragments, then the endsof the DNAs were blunted, dA-tailed and ligated with the premethylated adapters. Then the ligated DNAs were bisulfite-converted and amplified. As for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted from the postimplantation embryos using RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen), and RNA sequencing libraries were constructed under the standard protocol of illumina. The quality-ensured libraries were used for pair-ended deep sequencing on Illumina HiSeq2000 Sequencer.",,,,,,,,,,,,"Illumina CASAVA version 1.8 were used to the basecalling.;	Reads were trimmed to remove the adapter sequences and low quality bases.;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, bisulfite-converted reads were aligned to the reference genome (hg19) using Bismark software (version 0.7.0). For the RNA-Seq samples, cleaned reads were mapped to the reference genome (hg19) using BWA tools (version 0.6.2-r126).;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, the DNA methylation levels of the cytosines (in CpG, CHH or CHG context) were estimated using comstomized Perl scripts. While the genes expression levels were calculated using the comtomized Perl scripts.;	Genome_build: hg19;	Supplementary_files_format_and_content: For RRBS and WGBS samples, the processed txt files include the DNA methylation levels of cytosines in CpG, CHH and CHG context. Bisulfite conversion was performed under the manufacturerâ€™s instructions of the MethyCode DNA Methylation Kit (Invitrogen) with minor modification, the converted DNAs were enriched by two rounds of PCR amplifications and size-selected after running 12% native polyacrylamide TBE gel. For WGBS samples, DNAs isolated from the embryos were sonicated into small fragments, then the endsof the DNAs were blunted, dA-tailed and ligated with the premethylated adapters. Then the ligated DNAs were bisulfite-converted and amplified. As for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted from the postimplantation embryos using RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen), and RNA sequencing libraries were constructed under the standard protocol of illumina. The quality-ensured libraries were used for pair-ended deep sequencing on Illumina HiSeq2000 Sequencer.",,,,,,,,,,,,"Illumina CASAVA version 1.8 were used to the basecalling.;	Reads were trimmed to remove the adapter sequences and low quality bases.;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, bisulfite-converted reads were aligned to the reference genome (hg19) using Bismark software (version 0.7.0). For the RNA-Seq samples, cleaned reads were mapped to the reference genome (hg19) using BWA tools (version 0.6.2-r126).;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, the DNA methylation levels of the cytosines (in CpG, CHH or CHG context) were estimated using comstomized Perl scripts. While the genes expression levels were calculated using the comtomized Perl scripts.;	Genome_build: hg19;	Supplementary_files_format_and_content: For RRBS and WGBS samples, the processed txt files include the DNA methylation levels of cytosines in CpG, CHH and CHG context. or embryos were directely picked into the lysis buffer which contained protease to release the naked DNAs. For WGBS samples, genomic DNAs were extracted from the embryos using the Dneasy Blood & Tissue Kit (Qiagen). And for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted using the RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen).;	For RRBS samples, cells were picked into the lysis buffer to release naked DNA; then the released DNAs were digested with MspI, then filled-in and tailed with an extra ""A"" , then ligated with Illumina indexed adaptors. Bisulfite conversion was performed under the manufacturerâ€™s instructions of the MethyCode DNA Methylation Kit (Invitrogen) with minor modification, the converted DNAs were enriched by two rounds of PCR amplifications and size-selected after running 12% native polyacrylamide TBE gel. For WGBS samples, DNAs isolated from the embryos were sonicated into small fragments, then the endsof the DNAs were blunted, dA-tailed and ligated with the premethylated adapters. Then the ligated DNAs were bisulfite-converted and amplified. As for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted from the postimplantation embryos using RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen), and RNA sequencing libraries were constructed under the standard protocol of illumina. The quality-ensured libraries were used for pair-ended deep sequencing on Illumina HiSeq2000 Sequencer.",,,,,,,,,,,,"Illumina CASAVA version 1.8 were used to the basecalling.;	Reads were trimmed to remove the adapter sequences and low quality bases.;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, bisulfite-converted reads were aligned to the reference genome (hg19) using Bismark software (version 0.7.0). For the RNA-Seq samples, cleaned reads were mapped to the reference genome (hg19) using BWA tools (version 0.6.2-r126).;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, the DNA methylation levels of the cytosines (in CpG, CHH or CHG context) were estimated using comstomized Perl scripts. While the genes expression levels were calculated using the comtomized Perl scripts.;	Genome_build: hg19;	Supplementary_files_format_and_content: For RRBS and WGBS samples, the processed txt files include the DNA methylation levels of cytosines in CpG, CHH and CHG context. Bisulfite conversion was performed under the manufacturerâ€™s instructions of the MethyCode DNA Methylation Kit (Invitrogen) with minor modification, the converted DNAs were enriched by two rounds of PCR amplifications and size-selected after running 12% native polyacrylamide TBE gel. For WGBS samples, DNAs isolated from the embryos were sonicated into small fragments, then the endsof the DNAs were blunted, dA-tailed and ligated with the premethylated adapters. Then the ligated DNAs were bisulfite-converted and amplified. As for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted from the postimplantation embryos using RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen), and RNA sequencing libraries were constructed under the standard protocol of illumina. The quality-ensured libraries were used for pair-ended deep sequencing on Illumina HiSeq2000 Sequencer.",,,,,,,,,,,,"Illumina CASAVA version 1.8 were used to the basecalling.;	Reads were trimmed to remove the adapter sequences and low quality bases.;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, bisulfite-converted reads were aligned to the reference genome (hg19) using Bismark software (version 0.7.0). For the RNA-Seq samples, cleaned reads were mapped to the reference genome (hg19) using BWA tools (version 0.6.2-r126).;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, the DNA methylation levels of the cytosines (in CpG, CHH or CHG context) were estimated using comstomized Perl scripts. While the genes expression levels were calculated using the comtomized Perl scripts.;	Genome_build: hg19;	Supplementary_files_format_and_content: For RRBS and WGBS samples, the processed txt files include the DNA methylation levels of cytosines in CpG, CHH and CHG context. Bisulfite conversion was performed under the manufacturerâ€™s instructions of the MethyCode DNA Methylation Kit (Invitrogen) with minor modification, the converted DNAs were enriched by two rounds of PCR amplifications and size-selected after running 12% native polyacrylamide TBE gel. For WGBS samples, DNAs isolated from the embryos were sonicated into small fragments, then the endsof the DNAs were blunted, dA-tailed and ligated with the premethylated adapters. Then the ligated DNAs were bisulfite-converted and amplified. As for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted from the postimplantation embryos using RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen), and RNA sequencing libraries were constructed under the standard protocol of illumina. The quality-ensured libraries were used for pair-ended deep sequencing on Illumina HiSeq2000 Sequencer.",,,,,,,,,,,,"Illumina CASAVA version 1.8 were used to the basecalling.;	Reads were trimmed to remove the adapter sequences and low quality bases.;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, bisulfite-converted reads were aligned to the reference genome (hg19) using Bismark software (version 0.7.0). For the RNA-Seq samples, cleaned reads were mapped to the reference genome (hg19) using BWA tools (version 0.6.2-r126).;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, the DNA methylation levels of the cytosines (in CpG, CHH or CHG context) were estimated using comstomized Perl scripts. While the genes expression levels were calculated using the comtomized Perl scripts.;	Genome_build: hg19;	Supplementary_files_format_and_content: For RRBS and WGBS samples, the processed txt files include the DNA methylation levels of cytosines in CpG, CHH and CHG context. Bisulfite conversion was performed under the manufacturerâ€™s instructions of the MethyCode DNA Methylation Kit (Invitrogen) with minor modification, the converted DNAs were enriched by two rounds of PCR amplifications and size-selected after running 12% native polyacrylamide TBE gel. For WGBS samples, DNAs isolated from the embryos were sonicated into small fragments, then the endsof the DNAs were blunted, dA-tailed and ligated with the premethylated adapters. Then the ligated DNAs were bisulfite-converted and amplified. As for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted from the postimplantation embryos using RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen), and RNA sequencing libraries were constructed under the standard protocol of illumina. The quality-ensured libraries were used for pair-ended deep sequencing on Illumina HiSeq2000 Sequencer.",,,,,,,,,,,,"Illumina CASAVA version 1.8 were used to the basecalling.;	Reads were trimmed to remove the adapter sequences and low quality bases.;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, bisulfite-converted reads were aligned to the reference genome (hg19) using Bismark software (version 0.7.0). For the RNA-Seq samples, cleaned reads were mapped to the reference genome (hg19) using BWA tools (version 0.6.2-r126).;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, the DNA methylation levels of the cytosines (in CpG, CHH or CHG context) were estimated using comstomized Perl scripts. While the genes expression levels were calculated using the comtomized Perl scripts.;	Genome_build: hg19;	Supplementary_files_format_and_content: For RRBS and WGBS samples, the processed txt files include the DNA methylation levels of cytosines in CpG, CHH and CHG context. Bisulfite conversion was performed under the manufacturerâ€™s instructions of the MethyCode DNA Methylation Kit (Invitrogen) with minor modification, the converted DNAs were enriched by two rounds of PCR amplifications and size-selected after running 12% native polyacrylamide TBE gel. For WGBS samples, DNAs isolated from the embryos were sonicated into small fragments, then the endsof the DNAs were blunted, dA-tailed and ligated with the premethylated adapters. Then the ligated DNAs were bisulfite-converted and amplified. As for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted from the postimplantation embryos using RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen), and RNA sequencing libraries were constructed under the standard protocol of illumina. The quality-ensured libraries were used for pair-ended deep sequencing on Illumina HiSeq2000 Sequencer.",,,,,,,,,,,,"Illumina CASAVA version 1.8 were used to the basecalling.;	Reads were trimmed to remove the adapter sequences and low quality bases.;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, bisulfite-converted reads were aligned to the reference genome (hg19) using Bismark software (version 0.7.0). For the RNA-Seq samples, cleaned reads were mapped to the reference genome (hg19) using BWA tools (version 0.6.2-r126).;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, the DNA methylation levels of the cytosines (in CpG, CHH or CHG context) were estimated using comstomized Perl scripts. While the genes expression levels were calculated using the comtomized Perl scripts.;	Genome_build: hg19;	Supplementary_files_format_and_content: For RRBS and WGBS samples, the processed txt files include the DNA methylation levels of cytosines in CpG, CHH and CHG context. or embryos were directely picked into the lysis buffer which contained protease to release the naked DNAs. For WGBS samples, genomic DNAs were extracted from the embryos using the Dneasy Blood & Tissue Kit (Qiagen). And for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted using the RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen).;	For RRBS samples, cells were picked into the lysis buffer to release naked DNA; then the released DNAs were digested with MspI, then filled-in and tailed with an extra ""A"" , then ligated with Illumina indexed adaptors. Bisulfite conversion was performed under the manufacturerâ€™s instructions of the MethyCode DNA Methylation Kit (Invitrogen) with minor modification, the converted DNAs were enriched by two rounds of PCR amplifications and size-selected after running 12% native polyacrylamide TBE gel. For WGBS samples, DNAs isolated from the embryos were sonicated into small fragments, then the endsof the DNAs were blunted, dA-tailed and ligated with the premethylated adapters. Then the ligated DNAs were bisulfite-converted and amplified. As for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted from the postimplantation embryos using RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen), and RNA sequencing libraries were constructed under the standard protocol of illumina. The quality-ensured libraries were used for pair-ended deep sequencing on Illumina HiSeq2000 Sequencer.",,,,,,,,,,,,"Illumina CASAVA version 1.8 were used to the basecalling.;	Reads were trimmed to remove the adapter sequences and low quality bases.;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, bisulfite-converted reads were aligned to the reference genome (hg19) using Bismark software (version 0.7.0). For the RNA-Seq samples, cleaned reads were mapped to the reference genome (hg19) using BWA tools (version 0.6.2-r126).;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, the DNA methylation levels of the cytosines (in CpG, CHH or CHG context) were estimated using comstomized Perl scripts. While the genes expression levels were calculated using the comtomized Perl scripts.;	Genome_build: hg19;	Supplementary_files_format_and_content: For RRBS and WGBS samples, the processed txt files include the DNA methylation levels of cytosines in CpG, CHH and CHG context. Bisulfite conversion was performed under the manufacturerâ€™s instructions of the MethyCode DNA Methylation Kit (Invitrogen) with minor modification, the converted DNAs were enriched by two rounds of PCR amplifications and size-selected after running 12% native polyacrylamide TBE gel. For WGBS samples, DNAs isolated from the embryos were sonicated into small fragments, then the endsof the DNAs were blunted, dA-tailed and ligated with the premethylated adapters. Then the ligated DNAs were bisulfite-converted and amplified. As for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted from the postimplantation embryos using RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen), and RNA sequencing libraries were constructed under the standard protocol of illumina. The quality-ensured libraries were used for pair-ended deep sequencing on Illumina HiSeq2000 Sequencer.",,,,,,,,,,,,"Illumina CASAVA version 1.8 were used to the basecalling.;	Reads were trimmed to remove the adapter sequences and low quality bases.;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, bisulfite-converted reads were aligned to the reference genome (hg19) using Bismark software (version 0.7.0). For the RNA-Seq samples, cleaned reads were mapped to the reference genome (hg19) using BWA tools (version 0.6.2-r126).;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, the DNA methylation levels of the cytosines (in CpG, CHH or CHG context) were estimated using comstomized Perl scripts. While the genes expression levels were calculated using the comtomized Perl scripts.;	Genome_build: hg19;	Supplementary_files_format_and_content: For RRBS and WGBS samples, the processed txt files include the DNA methylation levels of cytosines in CpG, CHH and CHG context. samples, cells or embryos were directely picked into the lysis buffer which contained protease to release the naked DNAs. For WGBS samples, genomic DNAs were extracted from the embryos using the Dneasy Blood & Tissue Kit (Qiagen). Bisulfite conversion was performed under the manufacturerâ€™s instructions of the MethyCode DNA Methylation Kit (Invitrogen) with minor modification, the converted DNAs were enriched by two rounds of PCR amplifications and size-selected after running 12% native polyacrylamide TBE gel. For WGBS samples, DNAs isolated from the embryos were sonicated into small fragments, then the endsof the DNAs were blunted, dA-tailed and ligated with the premethylated adapters. Then the ligated DNAs were bisulfite-converted and amplified. As for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted from the postimplantation embryos using RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen), and RNA sequencing libraries were constructed under the standard protocol of illumina. The quality-ensured libraries were used for pair-ended deep sequencing on Illumina HiSeq2000 Sequencer.",,,,,,,,,,,,"Illumina CASAVA version 1.8 were used to the basecalling.;	Reads were trimmed to remove the adapter sequences and low quality bases.;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, bisulfite-converted reads were aligned to the reference genome (hg19) using Bismark software (version 0.7.0). For the RNA-Seq samples, cleaned reads were mapped to the reference genome (hg19) using BWA tools (version 0.6.2-r126).;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, the DNA methylation levels of the cytosines (in CpG, CHH or CHG context) were estimated using comstomized Perl scripts. While the genes expression levels were calculated using the comtomized Perl scripts.;	Genome_build: hg19;	Supplementary_files_format_and_content: For RRBS and WGBS samples, the processed txt files include the DNA methylation levels of cytosines in CpG, CHH and CHG context. Bisulfite conversion was performed under the manufacturerâ€™s instructions of the MethyCode DNA Methylation Kit (Invitrogen) with minor modification, the converted DNAs were enriched by two rounds of PCR amplifications and size-selected after running 12% native polyacrylamide TBE gel. For WGBS samples, DNAs isolated from the embryos were sonicated into small fragments, then the endsof the DNAs were blunted, dA-tailed and ligated with the premethylated adapters. Then the ligated DNAs were bisulfite-converted and amplified. As for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted from the postimplantation embryos using RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen), and RNA sequencing libraries were constructed under the standard protocol of illumina. The quality-ensured libraries were used for pair-ended deep sequencing on Illumina HiSeq2000 Sequencer.",,,,,,,,,,,,"Illumina CASAVA version 1.8 were used to the basecalling.;	Reads were trimmed to remove the adapter sequences and low quality bases.;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, bisulfite-converted reads were aligned to the reference genome (hg19) using Bismark software (version 0.7.0). For the RNA-Seq samples, cleaned reads were mapped to the reference genome (hg19) using BWA tools (version 0.6.2-r126).;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, the DNA methylation levels of the cytosines (in CpG, CHH or CHG context) were estimated using comstomized Perl scripts. While the genes expression levels were calculated using the comtomized Perl scripts.;	Genome_build: hg19;	Supplementary_files_format_and_content: For RRBS and WGBS samples, the processed txt files include the DNA methylation levels of cytosines in CpG, CHH and CHG context. Bisulfite conversion was performed under the manufacturerâ€™s instructions of the MethyCode DNA Methylation Kit (Invitrogen) with minor modification, the converted DNAs were enriched by two rounds of PCR amplifications and size-selected after running 12% native polyacrylamide TBE gel. For WGBS samples, DNAs isolated from the embryos were sonicated into small fragments, then the endsof the DNAs were blunted, dA-tailed and ligated with the premethylated adapters. Then the ligated DNAs were bisulfite-converted and amplified. As for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted from the postimplantation embryos using RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen), and RNA sequencing libraries were constructed under the standard protocol of illumina. The quality-ensured libraries were used for pair-ended deep sequencing on Illumina HiSeq2000 Sequencer.",,,,,,,,,,,,"Illumina CASAVA version 1.8 were used to the basecalling.;	Reads were trimmed to remove the adapter sequences and low quality bases.;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, bisulfite-converted reads were aligned to the reference genome (hg19) using Bismark software (version 0.7.0). For the RNA-Seq samples, cleaned reads were mapped to the reference genome (hg19) using BWA tools (version 0.6.2-r126).;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, the DNA methylation levels of the cytosines (in CpG, CHH or CHG context) were estimated using comstomized Perl scripts. While the genes expression levels were calculated using the comtomized Perl scripts.;	Genome_build: hg19;	Supplementary_files_format_and_content: For RRBS and WGBS samples, the processed txt files include the DNA methylation levels of cytosines in CpG, CHH and CHG context. And for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted using the RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen).;	For RRBS samples, cells were picked into the lysis buffer to release naked DNA; then the released DNAs were digested with MspI, then filled-in and tailed with an extra ""A"" , then ligated with Illumina indexed adaptors. Bisulfite conversion was performed under the manufacturerâ€™s instructions of the MethyCode DNA Methylation Kit (Invitrogen) with minor modification, the converted DNAs were enriched by two rounds of PCR amplifications and size-selected after running 12% native polyacrylamide TBE gel. For WGBS samples, DNAs isolated from the embryos were sonicated into small fragments, then the endsof the DNAs were blunted, dA-tailed and ligated with the premethylated adapters. Then the ligated DNAs were bisulfite-converted and amplified. As for the RNA-Seq samples, total RNAs were extracted from the postimplantation embryos using RNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen), and RNA sequencing libraries were constructed under the standard protocol of illumina. The quality-ensured libraries were used for pair-ended deep sequencing on Illumina HiSeq2000 Sequencer.",,,,,,,,,,,,"Illumina CASAVA version 1.8 were used to the basecalling.;	Reads were trimmed to remove the adapter sequences and low quality bases.;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, bisulfite-converted reads were aligned to the reference genome (hg19) using Bismark software (version 0.7.0). For the RNA-Seq samples, cleaned reads were mapped to the reference genome (hg19) using BWA tools (version 0.6.2-r126).;	For RRBS and WGBS samples, the DNA methylation levels of the cytosines (in CpG, CHH or CHG context) were estimated using comstomized Perl scripts. While the genes expression levels were calculated using the comtomized Perl scripts.;	Genome_build: hg19;	Supplementary_files_format_and_content: For RRBS and WGBS samples, the processed txt files include the DNA methylation levels of cytosines in CpG, CHH and CHG context. For WGBS samples, DNAs isolated from the embryos were sonicated into small fragments, then the endsof the DNAs were blunted, dA-tailed and ligated with the premethylated adapters.
